Beijing Road Incident: Those Arrested Were Not Tried Yesterday 121

Trial Procedure Issues Arise

Resolution Needed Before Proceeding

On the morning of the 8th, Chinese and Western detectives from the Laozao Police Station arrested four students from other provinces, Liu Zhiye, Wang Kuo-chih, Yan Jen-min, and Chen Ho-ching, at the Ningpo Native Place Association on Tibet Road for possessing reactionary leaflets. Subsequently, more people tried to enter the Beijing Grand Theater on Beijing Road and were arrested, including three workers, Tan Chen-chang, Cheng Lu-hsi, and Chen San-tai. At the time, Chang Chen-cheng was arrested for taking pictures of Liu Yi-ching, who was shot and killed during the disturbance. In the afternoon of the same day, Chen Mo-ke, also known as Chen Chung-hao, was found in possession of reactionary leaflets on Metherest Road by the Gordon Road Police Station and was arrested. All were transferred to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court for preliminary interrogation the next day, and an order was issued to detain them for further interrogation. The case was originally scheduled to continue yesterday morning, so the Laozao and Gordon Road Police Stations summoned witnesses and escorted Liu Zhiye and the other nine people to the waiting room of the Second Court of the High Court at around 9:00 AM. The Chinese and Western detectives in charge of the case also brought all the leaflets they had seized. The leaflets were almost all colors, red and green, and were quite eye-catching. Half an hour later, Criminal Judge Song Yuan appeared and ordered the defendants to be brought forward. Lawyer Bo Liang, who represented the police station in the prosecution, was about to stand up and make a statement when Judge Song declared that the case had been scheduled for trial today, but a trial procedure issue has now arisen, so it cannot proceed today. It must be resolved before the trial can begin. After the announcement, he amended the case docket to postpone the trial and ordered the police to escort the defendants back to the police station for detention.

Young Man Hurrying with Paper 122

Searched Because He Was Suspicious

Turned Out to Be Reactionary Propaganda

Hua Sheng, a Western detective from the Gordon Road Police Station, was passing Haifang Road at 6:30 AM on the morning of the previous day when he saw a young man carrying a bundle of paper, hurrying from east to west. Hua Sheng suspected something was wrong and stopped him for inspection. It turned out that the paper he was carrying was all reactionary propaganda. He was taken back to the police station. Under questioning, he said his name was Wan Chun-yu, 26 years old, from Wuhu, Anhui, and lived in a straw hut on Singapore Road. The detective immediately ordered a Chinese detective to accompany Wan to his residence to search it. Although they searched according to the address provided, they could not find anything. At 9:00 AM yesterday morning, he was prosecuted in the High Court for counter-revolutionary crimes. Judge Song opened a court for preliminary hearing. Police lawyer Bo Liang stated the case, and Detective Hua Sheng reported the circumstances of the defendant's arrest. Judge Song first asked him his name, age, and place of origin, and then asked him about the origin of the leaflets. Wan Chun-yu confessed that the leaflets were given to him by a fellow villager, Hu Ming-xing, the day before yesterday afternoon and instructed him to send them to the entrance of the Cade Road Cinema at 6:00 AM yesterday morning and hand them over to a person wearing a velvet hat and holding a silk handkerchief. Therefore, he sent them yesterday morning, but when he arrived at the entrance of the cinema, there was no one like Hu said, so he had to carry the leaflets back and was arrested on the way. He met Hu Ming-xing at Qunzhi University last year. After obtaining the confession, Judge Song ordered the defendant to be detained for further interrogation.

The Problem of the Unworthy Student's Posthumous Works 123

Ended inconclusively

All Not Accepted

Novelist Xiang Kairan (i.e., the Unworthy Student) was rumored to have died last year, so the Masses Bookstore printed the words "Posthumous Works of the Unworthy Student" on the advertisement of the National Skills Grand View book published by the company. Xiang Kairan then hired a lawyer to sue Fang Dongliang and Jiang Xia-hun of the Masses Bookstore. The former Provisional Court once held a hearing, which has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, it was time for another hearing. Judge Sun Yuan of the Special Zone District Court took the seat. The plaintiff Xiang Kairan and his lawyer did not appear in court. Defendant lawyer Zhang Chongding then presented Xiang Kairan's original manuscript, bills, advertisements, etc., proving that the National Skills Grand View book was indeed written by Xiang Kairan and was not a fake. As for the rumor that Xiang Kairan had died, all the tabloids at the time had records. At this point, he submitted the Crystal News, etc. for inspection. After inspecting it, Judge Sun said that Lawyer Zhang had raised a counterclaim in the previous court hearing, suing Xiang Kairan for fraud and false accusation. Now that the part of the lawsuit has been clarified, whether to continue pursuing the counterclaim. Lawyer Zhang listened and consulted with the defendant. At first, he did not agree to close the case, but after Lawyer Zhang's persuasion, he agreed to withdraw the counterclaim. Judge Sun then ruled that the plaintiff in this case had not appeared in court after being formally summoned, nor had he appointed a lawyer to appear on his behalf. According to the Criminal Procedure Law, it should be regarded as a withdrawal of the lawsuit. It is announced that this case will not be accepted. Regarding the counterclaim, according to the lawyer's application to withdraw it in the presence of the defendant, and the defendant has no objection, it should also be approved and announced that it will not be accepted.

Request to Dispatch Warships to Patrol Areas Under County Jurisdiction 124

The Shanghai County Government sent a letter yesterday to the First District Department of the Jiangsu Waterborne Provincial Public Security Team, stating: "Regarding the proposal by the district chiefs at the Second District Administration Meeting of our county on the eleventh of this month, requesting the county government to send a letter to the First District Department of the Waterborne Public Security Team to dispatch warships to patrol the areas under the county's jurisdiction to strengthen public security, it was discussed and resolved to proceed accordingly. We hereby request your district chief to investigate and immediately dispatch patrol warships to patrol the areas under the county's jurisdiction to deter and strengthen public security."

山东会馆之借用与使用问题 (The Issue of Lending and Using the Shandong Guild Hall)

同乡会与会馆之讼 (The Lawsuit Between the Native Place Association and the Guild Hall)

候会计师查明再核 (Awaiting Verification by an Accountant for Further Review)

The Shandong Native Place Association previously hired a lawyer as a representative to sue the Shandong Guild Hall in the French Concession court for refusing to allow the use of the guild hall building. The court approved the plaintiff's use of the guild hall building. Yesterday, the plaintiff's lawyer was summoned again, stating that after the court order, the defendants still refused to allow the plaintiff to move in and work, and requested the court to enforce the order. The defendant, the Shandong Guild Hall, also had a lawyer defending, stating that there were regulations for borrowing the guild hall premises. The regulations were presented for review, stating that if the plaintiff wanted to borrow the guild hall premises, they must abide by the rules before borrowing. The plaintiff's lawyer also stated that the use and borrowing were different. The current court order was for use, not borrowing, and requested clarification. Judge Gong Cheng ordered an accountant to verify and review the matter.

French Concession Tram Self-Combusts

电箱冒烟延烧木板 (Electrical Box Smokes, Flames Spread to Wooden Planks)

三十余辆四十分钟 (More Than Thirty Vehicles for Forty Minutes)

Yesterday afternoon at 12:30, French Concession tram F-112 on Route 10 from Lujiawan, while passing in front of the Enpaiya Cinema at Eight Immortals Bridge, suddenly had faint smoke coming from the electrical box under the first-class section in the rear. The driver initially did not notice and continued to drive forward. However, when passing the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Rue Amiral Bayle, the smoke became thick and with a loud bang, flames erupted, instantly spreading to the wooden planks inside the tram, turning them to ashes. The driver quickly stopped the tram, turned off the electricity, and pulled down the conductive iron rod on the roof. However, the fire continued to burn, so he telegraphed the company, which immediately dispatched several Chinese and foreign workers to remove the burning electrical box and douse it with cold water. The fire was extinguished after an hour. Tram F-117 on Route 2 from Xujiahui was then ordered to use the tracks on either side to tow the damaged tram back to the Lujiawan company for repairs. Fortunately, when the fire broke out, there were few passengers in the first-class section, and they all jumped out of the windows. There were more passengers in the third-class section, and they scrambled to escape, causing a great commotion and disorder. More than thirty trams were blocked and stopped, stretching from Rue du Consulat and Xinxiao Bridge to Avenue Joffre and Rue Tenant de la Tour, causing traffic to stop for forty minutes before resuming.

四行准备库劫案 (Four Banks Reserve Vault Robbery Case)

在汉又提回一盗 (Another Thief Brought Back from Hankou)

Fu A-Quan from Suzhou was also one of the thieves involved in the robbery of the Four Banks Reserve Vault of a large amount of currency. The Detective Feng Zhiming, Patrolman Bao Chengyu, Pang Yutang, and others from the Zhabei Police Station learned that the thief had fled to Hankou. They applied to the Special District Local Court, prepared an official letter, and went to Hanzhao to work with the local Public Security Bureau to arrest Fu A-Quan in Room 101 of the Pacific Hotel on Zhongshan Road in Hankou City. Of the stolen silver dollars the thief received, after spending some, there were still 1,170 yuan in banknotes from the Commercial Bank of China. The detectives boarded a riverboat and brought him back to Shanghai, arriving at the pier at 9:30 the night before. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Special District Court, where Judge Xu Jiashi opened the court for interrogation, and Chief Prosecutor Zhou also attended to perform his duties. First, Detective Feng reported the situation of the extradition from Hankou and the recovered stolen money. The Hankou Public Security Bureau temporarily detained the money because the documents from this side did not mention it, and planned to offer a reward from the money because of the 300 yuan reward for the arrest of the defendant. The remaining money was requested to be transferred to the case by writing another letter. Fu A-Quan confessed that he conspired with his brother Chen Ziqing to rob the bank's remittance, but he did not personally go to rob. Afterwards, Chen gave him 1,200 yuan, and when he heard that Yuan Genfa and others had been arrested, he fled to Hankou. Judge Xu approved the police station's request, ordered the defendant to be detained, and rescheduled the hearing to be combined with other cases.

月宫走电 (Yue Gong Electrical Leak)

The Yue Gong Hotel on North Sichuan Road is a four-story building with a thriving business. The night before, at around 11:00 PM, somehow the electrical box installed on the second floor suddenly had an electrical leak, with sparks flying and smoke swirling. Several guests were playing mahjong at the time, and they were terrified and rushed downstairs to escape. Fortunately, the police officer on duty at the Fifth District General Station saw it and reported it to the fire brigade, which rushed to the scene to extinguish the fire. The damage was minor. Tan Hanxi, the Guangdong accountant, was detained and transferred to the Judicial Section for review.

郑良斌盗卖轮船被扣 (Zheng Liangbin Detained for Stealing and Selling a Steamer)

Shanghai Hengping Company purchased the Fusheng steamer from Jardine Matheson in May of last year, renamed it Dazhen, and entrusted Jiaoyi Shipping Company to handle cargo solicitation and customs declaration matters. Recently, Zheng Liangbin, the shipping director of Jiaoyi Company, falsely claimed to be the owner of the steamer, stole and sold the steamer to someone named Gao, renamed it Antong, and planned to apply to the Ministry of Transportation for a license. Hengping Company discovered this, reported it to the Shanghai Shipping Association, and the chairman of the association, Yu Qiaqing, telegraphed the Ministry of Transportation to stop issuing the license and wrote to the Jianghai Customs Supervision Office to stop issuing the ship's license. At the same time, Ossen and Shan Yuhua, two lawyers, were hired to sue Zheng for stealing and selling the steamer in the Special District Local Court. However, after Hengping purchased the steamer, it was mortgaged to Yixing Qianzhuang, and the Qianzhuang had creditor rights to the Dazhen. Now that Zheng had stolen and sold it, Yixing also jointly sued with Hengping. They learned that the ship was currently docked outside the dock of the Hefeng Shipyard in Pudong and requested the court to issue a warrant to arrest the defendant and bring him to court for interrogation, and to impose a provisional attachment on the ship. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Ge Zhitan opened the court. Because the defendant Zheng Liangbin had not yet been arrested, the plaintiff's lawyer briefly stated the facts of the case. Judge Ge then ordered the defendant to be arrested for further questioning.

一週間捕房所获案犯 (Offenders Arrested by the Police Station in One Week)

Wenhui News reports that the Public Concession Police Station arrested a total of 244 offenders in various cases last week, including 70 with previous offenses. There were 10 kidnapping offenders, none of whom had previous offenses; 6 armed robbery offenders, 2 of whom had previous offenses; 6 pickpockets, 5 of whom had previous offenses; and 18 robbery offenders, 12 of whom had previous offenses.

砖船撞坏垃圾船 (Brick Boat Damages Garbage Boat)

Wu Erxizi, a garbage boat owner, after unloading two boats of garbage at Longhua Mouth around 6:00 PM the day before yesterday, hired the Yongde steamboat of Futai Company to tow the two empty boats north. When they reached the Pudong Bailianjing area, they encountered Wang Cai, a woman from Yancheng, sailing a boat loaded with green bricks from the Pudong side, veering towards Puxi and sailing horizontally. Zhao A-di, the captain of the steamboat, quickly pulled the horn and instructed them to give way, but the brick boat still sped straight ahead, causing a large hole in the empty garbage boat towed behind the steamboat. The boat immediately started leaking water. Xue Jinzhong, a member of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's water patrol team, encountered this while patrolling the river. Recognizing it as a boat collision, he arrested Wang. Just as he was about to take her back to the team, her crew members, Wang Jinyin and others, came out and acted barbarically, refusing to obey and attempting to flee. Xu, the team leader, heard about it and immediately dispatched Inspector Li Chenghua, leading Patrolman Wu Minshen, Team Member Zhang Maosen, and others on a speedboat to intercept and detain the cargo ship, along with Wang, her crew members Wang Jinyin and Wang Yuanfu, and the victim Wu Erxizi, and brought them back together. The team leader ordered them to be brought to a preliminary hearing, and then ordered them to be temporarily detained separately, instructing them to investigate and then review the matter.

顺泰里房客反对加租 (Tenants of Shuntai Lane Oppose Rent Increase)

Shuntai Lane in Zhabei is owned by Yue merchant Yu Xingyao. Last year, there was a dispute over water fees. Now, the tenants of the houses have received a notice from Tang Youwei, the lawyer representing the landlord, stating that the rent will be increased by 20% starting in April. 烟兑业整委会开会纪 (Minutes of the Meeting of the Tobacco Exchange Industry Reorganization Committee)

The Shanghai Special City Tobacco Exchange Industry Group Reorganization Committee held its second reorganization committee meeting yesterday afternoon. The meeting was held as usual. The chairman reported on the progress of the work, and then the following matters were discussed and resolved: (1) In accordance with legal procedures, the reorganization committee will send letters to the old associations to prepare registers and handle the handover. (2) It was decided that members should fill out membership application forms separately, and the members of the committee will be responsible for handling them separately within their original scope to simplify the process. (3) Chen Liangyu, Teng Zhixiang, and Zhang Songji were appointed to draft the articles of association of the guild and business regulations, which will be drafted immediately. (4) Regarding the price list for the sale of goods in the same industry, it was decided that the reorganization committee would first set the price list and distribute it to all members in the same industry for compliance. (5) Rush to handle the election procedures. (6) It was stipulated that standing committee members should take turns coming to the meeting to handle official business. Finally, other important cases were discussed, and the meeting was adjourned.

啜粥奇遇失踪妻 (An Unexpected Encounter with a Missing Wife While Sipping Porridge)

徐光来之一忧一喜 (One Worry and One Joy of Xu Guanglai)

Xu Guanglai, a Yancheng native living at No. 16 Tongji Road, Zhabei, makes a living by pushing a cart. His wife, Sun, is 23 years old and still quite beautiful. They have been married for several years and she has always been well-behaved. However, recently, she felt that her husband's income was too meager and she was often short of food. Unwilling to live in poverty, she became intimately acquainted with Xing Baoyu, a Funing native who trades in used goods. Xing has no wife and finds her young and beautiful, so he wants to take her as his wife. He gives her all the money he earns every day and coaxes her with sweet words, wanting to persuade her to run away with him. Sun is indecisive and her relationship with Xing is extremely close. When Xu is on the night shift, she often summons Xing to their home for secret meetings. Initially, Xu did not know. Last month, Xu passed by his home while pulling his cart and stopped by to see her, only to find his wife sleeping with a man in an intimate embrace. However, due to financial constraints, he pretended to be deaf and dumb and gently advised her, hoping that she would improve. But Sun did not repent. On the 18th of last month, Xu planned to take her back to their hometown. Unexpectedly, while passing the North Railway Station, she suddenly went missing. It turned out that Xing was waiting in the middle, and taking advantage of Xu's unpreparedness, she hired a rickshaw and went elsewhere. By the time Xu noticed, his wife was gone. He returned to his original place, crestfallen, and searched for her every day. Yesterday, he happened to pass Tongji Road, and because he was hungry, he went to a porridge shop to eat. Unexpectedly, his wife and Xing were also eating porridge there. He secretly reported it to the police, who arrested them and took them to the Second Precinct of the Fourth District. The case involves adultery and abduction, and they were ordered to be sent to the bureau for interrogation.

沈元生米船遭湖匪劫 (Shen Yuansheng's Rice Boat Robbed by Lake Bandits)

Shen Yuansheng, a boatman, was hired by a Shanghai rice merchant, Wu, to load 180 piculs of white rice in Wujiang and transport it to Shanghai. On the 8th of this month, Shen's boat sailed near the Guanyin Temple in Dianshan Lake. There, three or four bandit boats were anchored. Seeing Shen's boat approaching, they forced it to stop about a mile away. They fired several shots, injuring the crew and piercing the hull. The crew members panicked and had to stop. The bandits, carrying weapons, boarded the boat, extremely angry. They beat Shen and looted everything. They opened the cargo hold, saw the rice, and ordered Shen's boat to sail, with two bandit boats escorting it behind, heading towards Dianshan Lake. In the evening, they docked on the shore of Tai Lake, with Shen's boat in the middle, monitored by two bandit boats on either side. At midnight, they forced the crew to row on the bandit boats. The crew took advantage of the bandits' sleep, jumped ashore, and fled to safety. The next day, they took a small boat to Wujiang to report the incident. Yesterday, Shen's crew came to Shanghai and told Wu about the bandit robbery. Wu is trying to rescue the ship and has asked the water police to suppress the bandits. It is reported that several boats have been robbed by bandits and their ships have been looted in the Dianshan Lake and Tai Lake area recently, so everyone is vigilant and dare not transport goods through Tai Lake alone.

阿伯竟管弟媳妇 (Uncle Manages Brother's Wife)

周氏姘人而受苦 (Zhou Suffers from Adultery)

兄弟捉将官裏去 (Brothers Arrested and Taken to the Authorities)

Wang Shuming, a Yangzhou native living at No. 20 Chongfu Lane, Taiyangmiao Road, Zhabei, makes a living by pulling a rickshaw. His wife, Zhou, is 28 years old and works in a silk factory. The couple's relationship is not good and they often quarrel. Wang resentfully abandoned her. Zhou, relying on her own labor, had an affair with Li Changlin, a clothing maker from Funing, and often did not return home for days. Wang's older brother, Shugao, believed that his brother's wife's adultery was a disgrace to the family, so he confined Zhou in a room the day before, locked her with iron chains, did not provide her with food and drink, and often whipped her. Zhou could not bear it and shouted for help in the street. The police officer on duty heard it, went upstairs to check, and found her mentally exhausted and haggard. He immediately took her to the General Office of the Fourth District, learned the details, and ordered the police to arrest Wang Shugao and Li Changlin. After questioning them, he determined that the case involved criminal matters and sent them to the bureau for interrogation.

头颅轧碎 (Head Crushed)

郭小辅惨死 (Guo Xiaofu Dies Tragically)

Guo Xiaofu, an apprentice at the Huaming Mirror Factory on the Jilu Neighborly Lane in Shanghai County, which is owned by Huang Shengxiang and uses electricity to manufacture mirrors, died tragically. The factory is equipped with a motor engine and the business is thriving. The day before yesterday afternoon, Guo Xiaofu, also known as Guo Gaozi, a Jiangbei native who is 17 years old, was working on the machine, and carelessly crushed his head into the belt while transporting mirrors. He cried for help. Those in the factory saw this and immediately stopped the machine, but his skull had already been crushed, with blood and flesh all over the place, a terrible sight to behold. Guo was dying. The factory owner hired a car to take him to the Shanghai Hospital for treatment, but it was too late. He died on the way. The body was taken to the Xiying Public Office in Niumudi. The police from the Second Precinct of the First District summoned factory owner Huang Shengxiang. After questioning, the station chief ordered him to wait for review. He also ordered the local headman to report to the local court for an autopsy.

印花税局职员 下电车被汽车撞死 (Stamp Tax Bureau Employee Killed by Car After Getting Off Tram)

肇事之路仅四十六尺 (Road Where Accident Occurred Only Forty-Six Feet Wide)

汽车夫既查明无过失 (Driver Found Not at Fault)

工部局似应加以注意 (Municipal Council Should Pay Attention)

The day before yesterday at 12:30 AM, a car with license plate number 4472 was traveling east to west on Seward Road when Li Pengsun, an employee of the Stamp Tax Bureau at 84 Weihaiwei Road, got off a tram and crossed the road from north to south, colliding with the right headlight of the car and falling to the ground, bleeding profusely. A Chinese policeman with number 1865, also on the tram, got off to inspect the scene and reported it to the Huishan Police Station, which ordered detectives to take the injured person to the hospital for treatment. He died shortly after. The police station then took Li's body to the Ferren Road Morgue. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, Guo Wei, a prosecutor appointed by the Special District Local Court, arrived at the morgue to examine the body, ascended to the official seat, and heard the report from Western Police Chief Hua Sheng, who stated that the driver, Zhao Jinsheng, had been driving for three years and had no negligence. The police had measured the road where the accident occurred, which was only 46 feet wide, which was quite narrow. The accident was caused by the deceased's carelessness, and the driver was not at fault. Zhao Huahai, the head of the General Affairs Section of the Stamp Tax Bureau, stated that the deceased was a staff member of the bureau who contacted a cigarette factory every morning to discuss business. A telegram had been sent to his hometown, instructing his relatives to come to Shanghai to handle the funeral arrangements, and he would temporarily claim the body. Driver Zhao Jinsheng and Chinese policeman 1865 also submitted reports on the case. Prosecutor Guo Yu said that Li Pengsun had died as a result of being hit by car number 4472. Zhao Huahai was ordered to sign a guarantee to claim the body for burial.

六十岁旅客病毙 (Sixty-Year-Old Passenger Dies of Illness)

自称倪云卿 (Claiming to Be Ni Yunqing)

At the Yili Inn on Eight Mile Bridge Road (the southern section of Avenue Edward VII) in the French Concession on the evening before last (the 11th), an old man checked in, claiming to be Ni Yunqing, 60 years old, from Ningbo. Unexpectedly, after going to bed, he suddenly fell ill and died. When it was late in the morning, the waiter did not see Ni get up and went to call him but received no response. Touching him, he found the body cold. He immediately reported it to the police station, which ordered detectives to investigate. The deceased was found to have died of illness. He was wearing a gray gabardine short-sleeved jacket, gray crepe cotton pants, a coffee-colored velvet vest, a white cloth shirt, white flannel pants, coffee-colored socks, and a garter. He had no shoes and no belongings. No family members were found. The detective reported back to the police chief, and the body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall Morgue to await further instructions.

倒毙男尸 (Male Corpse Found Dead)

在金家弄年约三十余岁 (About Thirty Years Old in Jinjia Lane)

Yesterday morning, an unidentified male corpse was found dead in Jinjia Lane, Xian Gua Street, Nanshi. The police station of the First District ordered Lu Yongfa, the local headman of the 16th Pu, to report to the local court for an autopsy. 私刻图章冒领银洋被拘 (Illegally Carving Seals to Obtain Silver Dollars, Arrested)

Wang Dasheng and Xu Tingjia from Zhejiang colluded between the 4th and 6th of this month to illegally carve the seal of the Economic University on Jiangwan Road twice and fraudulently obtained 80 and 53 yuan in silver dollars from the China Post Office on North Sichuan Road. They escaped and spent the money. Yesterday, Tao Jinren, an employee of the post office, found out and reported it to the Hongkou Police Station, which dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to arrest Wang and Xu and put them in the police station to await investigation.

海味行加派会计师清理 (Seafood Store Appoints Additional Accountant for Liquidation)

Shareholders of the Yiji Seafood Store on Yanghang Street, Xiaodongmen in the French Concession, Liu Mingshan, Liu Dusheng, Liu Yusheng, and Liu Qingchu, jointly hired a lawyer to announce liquidation. Fang Shunyuan, a shareholder and manager of the store, came out to object and hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit in the French Concession Court. Yesterday, the plaintiff's lawyer stated that due to internal disputes in the Yiji Store, shareholders Liu Mingshan and others declared self-liquidation through a lawyer without the plaintiff's consent. The plaintiff did not object to the liquidation, but insisted that the court appoint another accountant to liquidate the store. The plaintiff strongly opposed the defendant's lawyer conducting the liquidation. The lawyer representing the defendant stated that the plaintiff was a shareholder and manager of the Yiji Store and that the store was completely used by the plaintiff alone to engage in speculative activities outside the store, resulting in losses of 70,000 to 80,000 yuan, which made it impossible to maintain the store. The defendants held a meeting to discuss, but the plaintiff refused to attend. Therefore, they had no choice but to temporarily appoint Liu Qingchu as the manager and hire their lawyer to liquidate the accounts, which was not inappropriate. Judge Gong Cheng approved the appointment of accountant Wu Ji to liquidate the accounts together with the lawyers from both parties and then review the matter for a decision.

船伙无辜被累 (Crew Members Unjustly Implicated)

吴淞商会设法营救 (Wusong Chamber of Commerce Seeks Rescue)

Zhang Xuezhi, a 43-year-old native of Xuzhou, has been working as a boat driver in the Su-affiliated anti-smuggling camp for more than ten years. His wife, Zhang, is 35 years old and has two young sons and a daughter, all living in the Li family's residence in Wusong for more than ten years. In recent years, the political situation has changed and Zhang has retired. He used his money to buy a customs boat, hired four crew members, and specialized in transporting firewood, selling it to various ports along the Yangtze River to make a small profit to support his family. Unexpectedly, at the end of October last year, Zhang's boat docked at the Liuhe Liumenjing port. Because the area is under the jurisdiction of Taicang County and theft cases have occurred repeatedly, the Floating Bridge Defense Corps mistakenly identified them as bandits. The boat and Zhang and the four crew members were sent to the Taicang County Government for questioning. Crew members Sun Shouhong and Wang Yulan were found to have committed crimes in the mainland and were sentenced to imprisonment by the county government. Zhang and the other two crew members have not yet been questioned clearly and have been detained in the county detention center for several months. After the incident, Zhang's family did not know the truth and, seeing that Zhang's boat had not returned for a long time, initially suspected that the boat had been overturned by the wind or robbed on the way. They sent people to search in all directions, but found nothing. Until the day before yesterday, they learned the truth. The Xuzhou-affiliated Shi Hu Native Place Association believed that they were indeed operating commercial ships and were law-abiding citizens. Because they mistakenly hired criminals as crew members, they were implicated and their families were helpless and extremely distressed. The association sent representatives, along with Zhang's wife and children, to the Wusong Chamber of Commerce yesterday morning to appeal, requesting the chamber to send a letter to the Taicang County Government to prove Zhang's innocence and release him to reunite with his family. Zheng Shushan, the chairman of the chamber, sent staff to investigate with various merchants in Wusong who had dealings with Zhang, and confirmed that he was a law-abiding citizen. He has already provided proof to the Taicang County Government and is seeking rescue.

巿工务局兴建董家渡菜塲 (Municipal Bureau of Public Works to Build Dongjiadu Vegetable Market)

The construction of the Dongjiadu vegetable market in this city has been planned for more than a year. Due to insufficient municipal funds, it could not be realized earlier. It is now learned that the Municipal Bureau of Public Works has determined to build it and has submitted it to the Municipal Government for approval. Bids will be invited for construction soon.

工部局 土木课长考察回沪 (Head of Civil Engineering Section of Municipal Council Returns to Shanghai After Inspection)

拟装烧毁垃圾新机器 (Plans to Install New Garbage Incineration Machines)

After arriving in Japan, he visited major cities such as Tokyo, Yokohama, Osaka, and Kobe, and conducted on-site inspections, which were very satisfactory. He has returned to Shanghai after completing his official duties yesterday and will report the findings to the bureau. It is now planned to implement the new plan in stages. The latest garbage incineration equipment is planned to be installed in two locations in the shortest possible time.

白囡变成黑囡 (White Girl Becomes Black Girl)

男女均被捉将官裏去 (Both Men and Women Arrested and Taken to the Authorities)

Shen Sujing (also known as Suqin), a 17-year-old local woman, lives at No. 85 Zixia Road, outside Dadongmen in Nanshi. Because of her fair complexion, people call her "White Girl." She has a romantic nature and was once a movie star, so the nickname "White Girl" is well-known in the area. Last year, she met Shi Axing, a 20-year-old Ningbo native who makes clothing at No. 33 Matianxing Lane, and they fell in love. Shi is poor, but because he loves Suqin, he gives all his wages and even pawns his fur coat to buy her clothes and various ornaments to please her. The couple's love is growing stronger. However, the woman is fickle and soon has other lovers, neglecting Shi. Yesterday afternoon at around 2:00 PM, Shi happened to see her at the Popular Cinema in Xiaonanmen. He called out her nickname, "White Girl," but she ignored him and glared at him. Shi was unable to vent his anger, so he dragged the White Girl out and punched her, knocking her to the ground. The woman's face was covered in mud. In an instant, the White Girl became a Black Girl. During the commotion, Sun Yunhe, the police officer on duty at the Second Post of the District, heard about it and came to arrest the man and woman, taking them to the Third Precinct of the First District for interrogation.

中国红会总医院之外评 (External Evaluation of the Chinese Red Cross General Hospital)

工部局卫生处长戴维士之赞许 (Praise from Davis, Head of the Health Department of the Municipal Council)

Davis, Head of the Health Department of the Municipal Council, accompanied by medical experts, visited the Chinese Red Cross General Hospital on Haig Road on the 3rd of this month. After spending half a day there, he believed that the hospital was well-managed. The hospital received a letter from Davis on the 8th, which said: "To Yan Jun, President of the Chinese Red Cross General Hospital, I extend my respects. I was pleased to visit your esteemed hospital last week and was graciously shown around by you and your colleagues, which brought me great joy. I learned that you have built a great new institution with limited financial resources. Your superior intelligence is admirable. Although the hospital buildings are mostly old, they are well-arranged and coordinated. Your hard work is commendable. Furthermore, I observed that the organization of each department is precise, the examinations are thorough, and the treatments are complete, which greatly benefits the people. This would not have been possible without your careful planning. I have reported the advantages of your hospital to the Municipal Council. I wish you a bright future and spring prosperity. Davis, Head of the Health Department of the Municipal Council, April 8." It is reported that since the hospital has been co-operated with the National Central University, President Yan Fuqing has carefully planned, hired famous doctors, and divided departments for treatment. The content has become more and more perfect. This time, it has been praised by foreigners, which is a great honor for the public hospitals in our country.

中国红十字会总医院 第一箇 领照之外籍女律师 (First Foreign Female Lawyer Licensed at the Chinese Red Cross General Hospital)

法国人路森堡 (French National Luxembourg)

Da Wan Bao reports that there is a foreign female lawyer who has obtained a license from the Ministry of Judicial Administration of China and can appear in court in the Special District Local Court and the Higher Second Branch Court. The lady's name is Luxembourg, and she is French. She has been practicing law in Shanghai for ten years. According to Xu Li, the first foreign lawyer to obtain a Chinese license, Ms. Lu is the first foreign female lawyer. Only Ms. Zheng Yuxiu has appeared in court as a Chinese female lawyer.

两少妇买鞋 被劫去钻戒三只 (Two Young Women Buying Shoes Robbed of Three Diamond Rings)

计值洋一千二百元 (Valued at 1,200 Silver Dollars)

Yesterday afternoon at around 8:00 PM, Zhang Qian, a young woman living at No. 27 in Jinjia Lane, Fangbang Bridge, in the city, and her girlfriend, Zhang Chen, dressed elegantly, drove to the Meifu Shoe Store at No. 671 Xiaohua Garden on Zhejiang Road to buy shoes. While the two women were choosing new women's shoes, their arms were half-exposed, and Ms. Qian's slender fingers were adorned with a diamond ring, its brilliance dazzling. Ms. Chen's fingers were adorned with two diamond rings, which were even more glittering, attracting the attention of thieves. When the two women were leaving, two thieves suddenly approached them, both wearing blue cloth short shirts, speaking with Shanghai accents, and looking like local hooligans. They pointed two guns at the two young women's chests and ordered them to take off their diamond rings. The two women, forced to protect their lives, let them take away the three diamond rings, valued at 1,200 silver dollars. Afterwards, they shouted "robbery," but the thieves had already disappeared into the crowd. They reported it to the Zhabei Police Station for investigation. The police dispatched detectives to investigate, but the thieves had already gone far away.

拐妇姚王氏抛弃上诉 (Abductor Yao Wangshi Abandons Appeal)

Yao Wangshi, a woman from Su, and Chen Yueying, a woman, previously carried seventeen-year-old Zhu Xingnan and eighteen-year-old Lu Jinnan on a Tongzhou seaship, intending to go to Tianjin. They were discovered by detectives from the Relief Association at the dock and escorted to the Water Police Station and transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for investigation. As a result, Yao Wangshi was sentenced to one year and four months of imprisonment, and Chen Yueying was found innocent. Zhu Xingnan and Lu Jinnan were temporarily sent to the Women and Children Relief Association to be raised, waiting for their families to sign for their return. The women's families have now petitioned to be allowed to take their daughters home. However, because the appeal period has not expired, they have not been approved to take them away. However, Yao Wangshi initially planned to appeal after being sentenced, but has now decided to abandon the appeal.

何有义私贩烟土 (He Youyi Illegally Sells Opium)

罚洋七百八十元 (Fined 780 Silver Dollars)

Lu Jinchen, Detective of the French Police Station, and Bao Tan Jiang Changwen and Gu Mingtong learned that He Youyi's home at No. 7 Huanghe Road was hiding opium and selling it secretly, violating the ban. They immediately went to confiscate 39 pounds of opium worth 1,650 silver dollars and took it to the police station. Yesterday, they sent it to the French Concession Court for investigation. He confessed that he was illegally selling opium. The Chinese and Western officials sentenced He to a fine of 780 silver dollars, and the opium was confiscated.

巿公用局业务报告出版 (Report on the Business of the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Published)

The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities publishes a business report every six months on the various businesses it handles. Since the establishment of the bureau, four issues have been published, which have been praised by readers. It is now learned that the issue for the second half of the 18th year has also been printed and published. The book is 260 pages long and is printed on high-quality Jiangnan Lianshi paper. The various businesses are described in detail and systematically, with no less than 80 statistical charts to assist in reference and explanation. The content is extremely rich and informative, and it is a must-have reference for those who study public utilities. (The price per copy is 1.5 silver dollars)

Further News on Wang Xiaoda's Kidnapping 125

The circumstances of Wang Binyan's son, Xiaoda, being kidnapped on Xinmin Road in Zhabei were detailed in yesterday's newspaper. It is reported that Mr. Wang has been managing the Zhabei Defense Corps and military supplies since the Jiazi year (1924), as well as various local public welfare projects, having advanced over 100,000 yuan. Besides mortgaging his residence and private property in Tongde Lane to the National Bank, Guangdong Bank, Cunde Money Exchange, etc., for six to seventy thousand yuan, he still owes several tens of thousands of yuan to private lenders, paying no less than 10,000 yuan in interest annually. Over the years, due to raising funds for interest payments, the directors of various charitable organizations sold part of the Pei Jiaqiao property, originally purchased with the advanced funds, to offset the debt. Last year, as there were no more assets to offset, the banks and money exchanges intended to sue in court. However, Chen Bingqian and others, mindful of Mr. Wang's financial losses due to public service, intervened to mediate, thus preventing the lawsuit. His enthusiasm for charity and public welfare is deeply appreciated in the local community. Currently, besides Mr. Wang requesting the authorities to conduct a thorough investigation, there is no further news on the case.

Municipal Public Works Bureau Focuses on Rectifying Traffic 126

The Municipal Public Works Bureau believes that traffic conditions in the city are becoming increasingly complex. Various regulations and traffic signals will only be effective if strictly enforced by traffic police. Therefore, based on the current traffic situation in the city, a letter has been sent to the Public Security Bureau, instructing traffic police to pay attention to the following points: (1) Traffic police should manage rickshaw parking areas to ensure orderly parking. (2) Street vendors and goods obstructing major traffic routes should be strictly prohibited. (3) Except in designated areas, vehicles are not allowed to park on both sides of busy roads. (4) Trams and buses should not stop or open doors at will before reaching the station, except in special circumstances. (5) Vehicles should not drive too fast when turning on roads. (6) No objects should be placed on sidewalks, obstructing pedestrian traffic. (7) Vehicles without licenses or tax permits should be confiscated, with particular attention to the Pudong area. (8) Vehicles that are incomplete or damaged should be punished according to regulations. (9) Motor vehicle drivers without driver's licenses are prohibited from driving and will be fined. (10) Auto repair shops and gas stations without licenses are not allowed to open or operate. (11) Various vehicles must not exceed the prescribed weight or passenger limits. (12) When impounding license plates or driver's licenses of vehicles violating regulations, the Fourth Section of the Public Works Bureau should be notified immediately by telephone (Nanshi 553) to prevent owners from fraudulently obtaining replacements. (13) Other vehicles are prohibited from parking near bus stops. (14) At all times and places, attention should be paid to whether the canopies, cushions, etc., of operating rickshaws are complete and clean.

Indoor Coffin Placement within the City to be Cleared 127

The Municipal Public Security and Health Bureaus, recognizing that indoor coffins are scattered in open fields within the city, have been exposed for a long time, inevitably spreading foul air and posing a threat of epidemics. They have jointly discussed and decided on measures to ban such placements, notifying coffin owners to relocate the burials. They have also convened a meeting of charitable organizations to discuss ways to bury ownerless coffins on behalf of the deceased. After considering the situation, it was decided to start with the densely populated and commercially prosperous areas of the North and South Municipalities. The Tongren Fuyuan Hall and Pushan Villa charitable organizations were tasked with selecting burial sites. Other districts will be handled in sequence. It is now known that these organizations have already buried ownerless coffins, totaling 204 in the South Municipality and 290 in the North Municipality, for a total of 494. The remaining coffins that have not been relocated by their owners will continue to be the responsibility of these organizations for burial.

Jinan University Welcomes Feng Yong 129

Zheng Hongnian Delivers a Welcoming Speech

Mr. Feng Yong, the owner and president of Feng Yong University in Liaoning, has led his students to participate in the National Games. Jinan University in this city, recognizing that both universities are renowned domestically for their excellence in sports, and also remembering that Jinan University’s student marching team was well received by Feng University during their visit to Liaoning last year, welcomed Mr. Feng and his students yesterday at 10:30 AM. The meeting was presided over by Mr. Zheng Hongnian, the president of Jinan University. In his welcoming speech, he stated that since the reform of Jinan University three years ago, there have been few welcoming events. This time, welcoming Mr. Feng is of great significance. Firstly, because of Mr. Feng's personality and family background, he could have occupied a very important position in local politics, or at least lived a life of wealth and honor. However, Mr. Feng focused on the most promising young people, painstakingly founding Feng Yong University. The eastern provinces are located between two major powers, and can only stand firm by restoring the national spirit. The fundamental way to restore the national spirit is through education. The Russian Kropotkin, a large landowner, diligently studied and wrote books, creating the philosophy of mutual aid, but Kropotkin's realization came after the age of fifty. Mr. Feng, at such a young age, already has such a thorough understanding. Secondly, because of Mr. Feng's arduous and outstanding spirit of running the school. Ten years ago, Yang Sisheng ran the Pudong Middle School in Shanghai, achieving excellent results. As for private universities, there was Chen Jiageng's Xiamen University, but even with Chen's vast wealth, he has recently requested government assistance. Only Mr. Feng, with his personal financial resources and energy, founded Feng Yong University, which has achieved the most success. Thirdly, because of Mr. Feng's spirit of armed defense of the country. When the Northeast Incident occurred last year, Mr. Feng led his students to organize an expeditionary army to resist the tyrannical Russians, personally going to the front line. His patriotic act was especially unique. Finally, he said that based on the sports achievements of the two universities, it can be jokingly said that in today's world, the only heroes are Gong and Cao. He hoped that the students of both universities would move from formal connections to a great spiritual unity. Then, Mr. Feng gave a speech, stating that he had many feelings about coming south this time. Today, he would only talk about the current situation and difficult circumstances in the Northeast. Few people in the country pay attention to the Northeast. The Northeast can be said to be in a state of sorrow and suffering. There is inevitably a gap between the central government and the local government, but in reality, the blame cannot be placed on the central government, nor can it be attributed to the local government. The ultimate responsibility still falls on the youth. If their thoughts, knowledge, physique are not sound, they cannot supervise internally or resist externally, and they are ashamed of the three Chinese characters. He hoped that all students would cultivate their character, work hard in science, and develop a true spirit, so as not to be left behind or corrupted, in order to consolidate the Northeast's frontier. His tone was extremely impassioned. He also said that after visiting Jinan University's various construction projects and teaching achievements, he would have a very good example to learn from when he returned to school. Later, teachers and students from both universities gave speeches and took photos in succession, ending with great joy. After the meeting, President Zheng Hongnian, in his private capacity, invited Mr. Feng and his students to a dinner at Hua'an. The basketball teams of the two universities also held a friendly match at the Sports Association.

Free Talk

A Smile 130

— Hai Ke

A: Why did you take off your hat to that girl? Do you know her?

B: I don't know her. It's just that the hat I'm wearing is my brother's, and my brother is very friendly with her.

Teacher: Children, do you know what wind is?

All the elementary school students could not answer.

Teacher: What? Doesn't anyone know?

Student: I know. Wind is air running urgently because it has important business to attend to.

A: You come back late every night. What does your wife say?

B: The difficulty is not knowing what to say. Because I have to think of new tricks every day, creating something out of nothing. I'm really running out of ideas.

A: Your son is so naughty. Why don't you beat him up?

B: It's just that my radio often breaks down, and he's the only one who can fix it.

Wife A: My husband always rests comfortably every night when he gets home, I always tell him to lean in the armchair and put his feet on the fireplace.

Wife B: You clever devil. You must have something up your sleeve.

Wife A: Yes. After he leaves, there are often one or two foreign money coins left in the chair.

Scattered Notes Welcoming Special Envoy Chu 131

— Yan Zi

Mr. Chu Minyi, a member of the Central Committee, is skilled in boxing and has been working for the revolution for nearly thirty years. He is indeed an important figure in the party and the nation. This time, he was ordered to go to Belgium to attend the World Expo. He set sail on the fifth of this month. The weather was clear and calm at the start, and those who saw him off were a sea of people, making it quite a grand occasion. Therefore, I will record what I saw that day with my pen.

Parting Words from Important Figures and Fellow Townsmen: Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Industry and Commerce, Li Shizeng, a member of the Central Committee, and Wang Xiaolai and more than ten others, as well as the Huzhou Fellow Townsmen Association, such as Qiu Shengnong, Lu Liankui, and Pan Yisheng, and dozens more, as well as Shao Rugong, the Secretary-General of the World Peace Association, gathered at the Baique Temple on Alabastine Road before dawn. There were more than twenty cars. Chen Shaolan, Su Xingheng, and others each held a send-off flag, hundreds of them, fluttering in the wind, tailing each other. The viewers along the way caused ten thousand people to empty their lanes. It was truly a grand sight.

Five-Colored Leaflets in the Flames Flew Across the Sky: Mr. Shao Rugong has a good relationship with Mr. Chu. He specially asked the art experts Sang Dongchen and Dai Jinsheng to make five hundred fireworks that produced light, which were lit along the way and soared into the clouds. The exploding Chinese and Western five-colored leaflets fluttered across the sky. Some fell into foreign warships, and the sailors picked them up and cheered. Because the leaflets contained phrases such as welcoming the Belgian Expo and long live all countries, they felt deep sympathy.

Mutual Responses Between a Million-Crack Firecracker and Military Bands: The Fellow Townsmen Association pre-purchased a million-crack firecracker, attached with a thousand skyrockets. When set off, the sound was like a string of pearls. The melodious military music enhanced the excitement.

The Default of the Pre-Chartered Launch: Shao Rugong sent Zhou Baozhi and Li Bingcheng, the staff of the Peace Association, to pre-charter two launches in order to tow the barges and carry the well-wishers to escort the departure. Unexpectedly, the pre-chartered launches did not arrive. It was already noon, and they were anxious. Just then, a Huzhou launch arrived at the port. Shao Rugong immediately called the launch boss and asked them not to turn off the engine temporarily, so they could tow the company boat of well-wishers and manage to catch up. Amidst the military music and flag shadows, they escorted Mr. Chu to board the boat and set sail. Mr. Chu took off his hat to say goodbye on the ship's rail. The waving of handkerchiefs and hats on the shore, as well as the applause, expressed a strong sincerity. It was truly an unprecedented event.

A Trip to Longhua 132

— Du Shaomei

In the third month of spring in Shanghai, men and women like to take trips to Longhua, for the peach blossoms are bright and the spring light is beautiful. On the fifth of this month, a former subordinate of my father, a certain Fang from the Material and Official Department, happened to come from Longhua, saying that the peach blossoms on the road were in full bloom. I happily took my younger sisters, Xiaomei and Youmei, to go with me. I also invited Mr. Wang Meiju, but he was unable to go due to other matters, which was a great pity. So, at two o'clock, I ordered the car to set off, with Fang as our guide. We went from Seymour Road to Jinji Bridge. In about a quarter of an hour, there were already many tourists by the bridge.

The Scenery Along the Way: Half a li away from Jinji Bridge is Jijiawan, Fang's house. Fang said that it would be better to stop here, otherwise it would be no different from clearing the way among the flowers. I agreed. So, we stopped the car. Fang was also worried that it would be difficult for us to walk, as I am sixteen years old, Xiaomei is eleven, and Youmei is only seven. We went to his house, and he served us tea. After a while, we walked out of Jijiawan onto Longhua Avenue. Along the way, children flew kites, and old and young picked wild greens. The elderly with yellow hair and the young with drooping hair were all enjoying themselves. Unexpectedly, we found a paradise in this bustling city.

The Great View from the Pagoda: There is a pagoda in Longhua, next to the Jingjing Temple. The temple is not large, but the incense is very popular. There are many tourists. The monks in the temple rely on this time of year. Youmei wanted to climb the pagoda. We climbed up the steps, which are very narrow. It is easy to go up, but difficult to go down. Leaning on the railing and looking into the distance, Fang said that the east of the pagoda is Pudong, the south is the Cement Factory, the west is New Longhua, and the north is the city of Shanghai. Xiaomei said that it is no different from the Chaoran Terrace. When we went down the pagoda, there was a child crying, because there were no railings on the stairs, and he was afraid of falling to his death.

The Flowers and Trees in the Wei Family Garden: After we were tired of visiting, we wanted to go home. Fang said that there is the Wei Family Garden here, which has very beautiful scenery. So, we entered a small bridge and went through a winding path to the garden. The garden is seventy acres in size, surrounded by a small stream. The flowers and grass are very lush, especially the pine trees, towering into the sky. There are many kinds of them. There are several graves in the garden, covered with pine trees, which is especially peculiar. There are also dozens of red maple trees, as tall as the buildings. It is truly a rare sight.

The Desires of the Local Elders: There are many peonies in the garden. When we entered the garden, a local villager in his fifties suddenly offered to guide us, emulating Mao Sui's self-recommendation. When he saw the peonies, he pointed to them as Chinese toon heads. There were also daffodils. Fang joked, "Is this leek?" Those who heard it laughed, and the villagers grumbled, meaning something else, like what the people of Hangzhou call peeling cucumbers, or what the people of Shanghai call knocking on the bamboo pole. I gave him four silver coins, and he thanked us and left. It was both pitiful and laughable.

Returning with Poems in the Setting Sun: After a while, the sun was setting in the west, and we were about to go home. We walked to Jijiawan, got into the car, and crossed the Jinji Bridge. There were even more tourists, similar to the scene at the ancient Gaoliang Bridge. So, I recorded it in a seven-character律詩 poem. The poem says: (Small note: car at Jinji Bridge, kites flying, wine flags fluttering. The incense has burned to the end, costing thousands of gold. The pagoda shadow soars high, like a jade strip. The willow color is green, and the spring color is transparent. The peach blossoms are bright, and the sun is beautiful. The silent lushness all contains smiles, as if sending the tourists home.) Xiaomei also has a poem: (The green willows are gentle, and the soft strands hang down. The peach blossoms are bright and beautiful. The seven levels of the pagoda reach the sky, silently making an appointment with Longhua for a later date.)

Wang Jiyuan's European Tour Farewell Painting Exhibition 133

— Qingkou

Mr. Wang Jiyuan, a well-known artist in the art world, resigned from his teaching position at the Shanghai Art College in 1926, immersed himself in research, and traveled extensively. He has traveled to the East four times and visited scenic spots in the country, collecting painting materials. His art has made rapid progress. All kinds of oil paintings, crayon paintings, ink paintings, and watercolor paintings of human bodies, landscapes, and still life are exquisite and profound. We have already seen them at the National Art Exhibition and the first Art Garden Art Exhibition.

Now, Mr. Wang will go to Europe at his own expense. His recent works from the past year will be on display at the Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association on Tibet Road from the 11th to the 14th of this month as a memorial exhibition for his European tour. I drove over to see it one day before the opening, and I was greatly amazed. Mr. Wang's style is very different from the past, combining fineness and boldness. His boldness is like the galloping of ten thousand horses, and his movingness is like the night cry of a cuckoo, making people reluctant to leave the venue. This shows the depth of the art's appeal. I will record it when I return.

April 10th last year was the opening day of the National Art Exhibition. April 10th this year is the opening day of Mr. Wang's solo exhibition. Although there was thunder and lightning and heavy rain, the audience still went in the rain. I like his watercolor sketches and new country paintings of Lai the most. Most of them are his friends, such as the painters Chen Baoyi, Pan Yuliang, Chen Chengbo, Jin Qijing, Liu Yanren, Wang Dilang, Deng Fen, and Zhang Chenbo, as well as Li Shizeng, a member of the Central Committee, Chen Bulei, a professor from Zhejiang, Zheng Echun, and celebrities such as Ye Yuhu. They have all marked Wang's works. The person in charge of the exhibition heard that pre-sale tickets had been sold in advance, so people competed to buy them, which is a good phenomenon for promoting new art.

Large-scale oil paintings, such as "Regret", "Mask", and "Seeing the Light Again", contain profound meaning. "Regret" depicts a naked woman wearing a silk robe, covering her forehead, turning her head upwards and looking back. The muscles are tense, with unspeakable secrets. It is indeed the largest and most moving work in the venue. "Mask" depicts the greed and vanity of human beings, who are enslaved by material things. A green mask covers their eyes, and their hands are wrapped in gold ornaments. They are interacting with two men in the background, which is a miniature of the dark society. It is probably the author's feelings. "Seeing the Light Again" seems to be a continuation of "Mask". It depicts a naked woman sitting by the window, bowing her head in repentance. Masks are discarded all over the ground, and she sees the light of the earth again. The purple-blue background contains infinite hope, which also shows the painter's hard work.

The small works, such as the sketches in Suzhou and Hangzhou, are even more brilliant. It is said that Mr. Wang can paint twenty paintings every morning and evening during his short journey, which can be said to be a divine skill. During this solo exhibition, art lovers should not miss it.

Preface to the Special Issue of the Completion Ceremony of the New Building of the Thai Chinese General Chamber of Commerce 134

— Zhu Zhaoxin

What I saw in the South Seas: seven or eight out of ten people coming and going are Chinese. If you don't ask who the rulers are, you won't mistakenly think it's your hometown. The Chinese in Thailand are more numerous than elsewhere. The land in Thailand is vast and the population is sparse, so they want to recruit immigrants to fill it. They love the Chinese race, so they especially like the Chinese to come, settle down, enjoy their customs, and live and prosper. The Chinese in Thailand are therefore growing in size. Many are farmers, many are workers, and many are merchants. The greatness of the commercial organizations is also unmatched. Last summer, I resigned from my official position and traveled south. When I arrived in Bangkok, I saw the newly built Chinese General Chamber of Commerce. It was magnificent and beautiful. President Huang Qingxiu extended a piece of paper and a pen and asked me to write a plaque. When I said goodbye, I wrote the four characters "Never Forget the Motherland" to encourage him. Half a year after I returned to China, President Huang sent a letter to inform me of the completion ceremony and that a special issue would be published as a memorial. He asked me to write a preface. I heard that the ceremony was very grand. The King and Queen of Thailand and local celebrities and envoys from various countries all attended. The grandeur of the event can be imagined, and the elevated position of Chinese merchants can also be understood. However, these things are not necessary to say. What I want to say is the two ends of the nationality treaty. Nationality is the easiest to obtain and the most difficult to obtain. For the natives, there is a reason to go out. For example, Lu Tong had a son named Tianding, which means to add one ding to the country. This is the natural result of obtaining nationality. There are parents who are not citizens of the country, but their children are born in this land, and they can also be registered as citizens. This is the result of the principle of jus soli. There are those who are born abroad, but naturalize according to bloodline, and still obtain the nationality of their parents. This is the result of the principle of jus sanguinis. There are those who live in a certain place for many years, and obtain the nationality of their place of residence at their own request. This is the result of their will. As for those who are neither born in the land, nor naturalized according to bloodline, nor have lived there for many years, they naturally obtain nationality after the permission of legal procedures. This is truly rare in the world. It only exists in Thailand's treatment of Chinese people. Once a Chinese person enters Thailand, Thailand regards them as citizens. There are inherent reasons for this, but the number of gains and losses for us may be questionable. If we think it is a loss, it is like when Chinese people go to the United States. It is already difficult to enter the country, let alone become a citizen. Because people of the yellow race, except for those born in the country, cannot enjoy the rights of citizens. It is as easy to obtain Thai nationality as picking up grass. If we compare this example with theirs, how can we not accept it? If we think it is a gain, then one more Thai citizen is one less Chinese citizen. However, our country's nationality law states that for citizens who go to other countries and their children who are born elsewhere, if they have not formally renounced their nationality, they are still citizens of China if they return at any time. When Japanese people go abroad to make a living, their government protects them, and even helps them obtain the nationality of other countries for the convenience of business. It is true that a country's population is too large, so there must be a place to settle them. The gains and losses of nationality cannot be discussed in general. Therefore, it is permissible for our people to temporarily obtain Thai nationality. When they return, they will be Chinese citizens. However, it is a pity that the Sino-Thai treaty has not been concluded, our country has no permanent consul in Thailand, and overseas Chinese cannot receive adequate protection. In terms of geography, Thailand is in the same continent as us. In terms of history, Thailand was our former vassal. In terms of race, the Chinese in Thailand have grown and merged into one. In terms of commerce, Chinese overseas in the whole Thailand involved. There is a close relationship between China and Thailand. How can there be no treaty for a day? Thailand has treaties with Japan, which is in the same continent, and with the white colonial territories that are in the same continent, but it has no treaty with the largest independent country in the same continent. What is the reason? The conclusion of the Sino-Thai treaty has not been realized. They say that the reason is that there have been many accidents in China for many years. How can we know that we are negotiating to revise the equal treaties with various countries? However, they deliberately postpone it. What they mean is not to despise China, but to fear China. According to the previous saying, the great power cannot tolerate it. According to the latter saying, the Chinese race is peaceful, why bother too much? We believe that after the treaty is signed, the friendly relations between China and Thailand will be strengthened, and the difficult problems faced by overseas Chinese in Thailand will be solved easily. This is what the governments of both countries are praying for. The country is to the people as parents are to their children. Ascending high, we know the longing of the son for his parents. Leaning on the gate, we know the concern of the parents for their son. The country does not abandon its people, and the people do not forget their country. They are no different from each other. The further away they are, the stronger their centripetal force. The sincerity of overseas Chinese to love their country is evident. Chinese merchants in Thailand built a guild hall and call it "Chinese", not forgetting their roots. In one fell swoop, the spirit of respecting work, enjoying the community, and loving the country is revealed. In the absence of a treaty to protect them, the spirit and ability of self-government are especially unattainable. Alas, how admirable it is! Spring of the 19th year of the Republic of China. Zhu Zhaoxin of Huaxian prefaced.

Heart's Warmth (169) 135

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Ten: Crimson Flames Soar, a Courtesan is Praised for Filial Piety; Red Carpet on the Ground, Meeting Famous Actors

Ruiyun and the others returned home. The eldest aunt said, "Oh dear, where did you go to see the play? There were several tickets with your name on them, requiring your personal presence. I asked the servants to help return them. They all said they couldn't find the place. What's this 'Moudeli' or whatever, opened in such an obscure location? We've lived in Shanghai for more than ten years, and we've only heard of Dan Gui, Tian Xian, and other teahouses. There's no such theater. One of the servants circled the main road several times but couldn't find it. I was scolding those good-for-nothings, wondering why they didn't send someone with you when you left earlier. They're just lazy. " Zuo Shichen secretly laughed upon hearing this, thinking, "Luckily, when we went, we didn't have Ruiyun take a chartered car. Otherwise, they would have been circling around trying to find Moudeli." But even if they had found the place, the doorkeeper wouldn't have let them in. Now that it's all over, there's no need to reveal it. Ruiyun was very happy that day. She actually got to comfortably watch the entire play from beginning to end without any interruptions, feeling very satisfied. At this moment, several younger sisters in the room wanted her to tell them everything about the play she had seen. Ruiyun put on airs and said, "This kind of play isn't like the old plays with gongs and drums in the old theaters, nor is it like the popular 'civilized plays' of today. It's a play that a group of students who studied in Japan wrote themselves when they felt like it. They only perform when they're in the mood. Even if you offered them tens of thousands of dollars, they wouldn't perform if they didn't feel like it." Fengyun said, "This is just another new play. It's not as good as the old plays. Old plays have singing. I like listening to the singing. Some of the old men sing really well." Then Fengyun began to hum "(I was originally) Wolonggang." Hanyun was about to listen to the story of the play and said, "Don't make noise. I know you can sing a few lines. If you want to be happy, you can sing a few more songs on stage tomorrow. Why did you argue with the huqin player and say he wasn't playing in tune?" Ruiyun then told them the name of the play, called "不如歸" (不如归; Buru Gui or "Better to Return Home"), which was a tragic play. In the later scenes, the Second Young Master said, "I'm going to cry." I said, "I never cry." Many people cry when they read novels and reach a sad part. I don't. But in the end, when it got to the sad part, I really did cry. Everyone in the theater, all the women, cried. Hanyun said, "If you're going to cry, then don't watch it." Ruiyun said, "The Second Young Master said the same thing, 'Let's go back.' But the more tragic it became, the more we wanted to watch it. It seemed like the more tragic it was, the more flavorful it became. It wasn't just us; no one in the whole theater wanted to leave." Just as she said that, they heard a lot of noise downstairs. Zuo Shichen said to Ruiyun, "What's going on? There's a lot of noise downstairs."

White粳 Rice Falls Short by Two Jiao... 秈元 Rice Also Turns Weak

Zhabei: Yesterday, very few boats arrived from the river, practically none, and local sales were very sluggish, almost stagnant. However, accumulated stock is substantial, and sentiment is poor. Merchants, seeing the market's sluggishness, are eager to sell, but buyers are few. Though anxious, it's no use. Therefore, although Northern 粳 Rice fell short by two jiao on the market, transactions still didn't pick up. The sluggish sales are the real problem. Yesterday, the flour market was unstable for all months, especially April and May, where sentiment was even more weak. For this month, actual sales are not picking up, and the market has been sluggish for a long time. Daily sales from Tianjin are less than 30,000, and the current stock is still 1.5 to 1.6 million. There are also foreign flour orders yet to arrive, totaling over 2 million bales. Therefore, during the transition period, Tianjin will naturally not inquire. As for May, because the difference with June is too great, it can be maintained when sales are strong. However, people now seem to be considering this, believing that the inverted situation will be difficult to sustain for long. The lack of confidence and the dumping of stock are due to this. However, because manufacturers of far-term new flour are unwilling to try dumping and inland gangs are still firm in their thinking, the price drop is still small. Based on this situation, it is predicted that later steps will likely lead to near-term suppression and far-term equalization. As a result, this month fell by one fen compared to the previous day, June fell by one fen, two li, five hao, June small five li, July small two li, five hao, August small five li, September unchanged, it is said.

Wheat Spot and Futures Markets Are Both Flat 150

Yesterday, the wheat futures market generally showed signs of stability for all months. For this month, the bulls and bears have largely reached an understanding, so there were few fluctuations. After the daily rise of new wheat in far-term months, sentiment has turned stable. However, this kind of new wheat price is already considered unusually expensive. If it were to be raised further, it would be too unrealistic. As a result, this month was higher by one fen compared to the previous day, June and July had no change, August was lower by one fen, and September was higher by one fen. The spot wheat market has become stable. There were rumors of a sudden and widespread surge a few days ago. Because local factories, seeing the purchasing by inland factories, intentionally raised prices to show resistance. Therefore, inland areas did not purchase, and the market became flat. Xuzhou wheat opened at five taels, one mace, eight fen. Nansuzhou wheat opened at five taels, one mace, eight fen. Bengbu wheat opened at five taels, one mace, eight fen. Shashi wheat opened at four taels, nine mace, two fen. Jiangxi wheat opened at four taels, nine mace, four or five fen, four taels, nine mace, two fen, four taels, nine mace, and four taels, eight mace, seven fen, for a total of 5,600 bales, purchased by local factories, it is said.

Soybean Market Temporarily Settled 151

Yesterday, the soybean market was flat. Prices were slightly weak, and Shanghai sales were not strong. Spot prices were the same as the near-term standard, both opening at five taels, four mace, five fen. Local interest was not good, and inland gangs were especially ordinary. The situation is temporarily settled. There were customer inquiries for futures bean cakes. Far-term cakes were perceived to be slightly firm. June was lower, opening at one tael, eight mace, four fen.

Silk and Tea Factory Exports to America Are Increasingly Smooth 152

Exchange Rate Turns Tight

Recently, the exchange rate has become firmer, and the US dollar has strengthened. At this time, the sale of Chinese silk to America has suddenly become smoother, and exports are increasingly smooth. Various American firms are very interested in the Shanghai factory products. However, the Shanghai stock of dried cocoons is limited, insufficient for silk reeling, and supply cannot meet demand. The attitude of the manufacturers is becoming firmer, and the market is becoming more attractive. Yesterday, 乾利 and others imported eighty bales of white factory silk into Shanghai. 伯興 imported eighteen bales of yellow reeling silk. Prices are becoming more firm, it is said.

1,440 bales of wheat and mung beans shipped from Changsha.

549 pieces of foreign cloth shipped to Tianjin.

155 boxes of tin foil shipped to Northern Tianjin.

3,200 jars of fermented bean curd shipped to Yantai Tianjin.

500 barrels of tung oil and crude oil shipped from Hankou to Shanghai.

2,200 tons of steel shipped from America to Shanghai.

200 pieces of Hubei official cloth shipped to Shanghai.

121 pieces of silk waste and yellow silk shipped from Yantai to Shanghai.

1,785 bales of beans shipped from Tianjin to Shanghai.

600 pieces of pigment shipped from Germany.

Hakodate Telegram: Dried scallops from the South Seas are selling well, and market prices have soared by fifteen or sixteen yuan.
