Group News 153

The Shanghai YMCA announced that the academic lectures initiated by the association have been held five times. All details have been reported in previous newspapers. The sixth lecture is scheduled for 3 PM this Sunday afternoon in the association's auditorium. The speaker will be Mr. He DeKui, and the topic will be "My Views on the Kemmerer Currency System Plan." Those who wish to attend should obtain admission tickets from the association, it is said.

The YWCA on Museum Road announced that the association's operations are expanding daily, and the original location is insufficient. It has been decided to move to the second floor of the 别发 洋行 on Nanjing Road. The location is in the center of Shanghai's commercial district, and the association site is very spacious. Mr. Wade Ben, manager of 别发 洋行, will donate 350 taels of monthly rent to the association. The association will move in on May 1st, it is said.

Business News 154

The Guanghua Bookstore on Fourth Avenue announced that the bookstore recently established a reading club. The methods are very complete and benefit general readers. Therefore, there are currently many people joining the club, truly an unprecedented grand event in the reading community. The membership methods and member benefits are briefly described below for reference by interested parties. Membership Method: Only a membership fee of five yuan is charged. After joining, members can enjoy the following benefits: (1) Book vouchers worth five yuan, (2) A copy of Guo Moruo's recently translated "Kerosene," (3) A long-term discount voucher, (4) A special discount voucher, (5) A "Mengya" monthly discount voucher, (6) A "Social Science Lecture" discount voucher, (7) A "Baerti Mountain Xunk Kan" discount voucher, and introduction benefits, etc. The bookstore has printed detailed regulations, which will be sent upon request, it is said.

The Sanyou Industrial Company announced that the company's products are excellent, durable, and welcomed by the sports community. Currently, athletes from the National Games are flocking to Shanghai, and the demand for all daily necessities is extremely high. Therefore, starting yesterday, sports shirts, pants, clothing, bathrobes, etc., will be discounted to show preferential treatment, it is said.

The Shanghai Commercial Press announced that since the bookstore began selling cameras at discounted prices, people from all walks of life consider them a timely and needed item, and many are taking the opportunity to purchase them. Various camera cases and accessories are mostly manufactured by the world-renowned German Zeiss Ikon factory. The lowest price is only 50% off. They are sold at the bookstore's distribution center and Hongkou branch. The discount period ends at the end of this month, it is said.

Theater News 155

The Penglai Grand Theater in Xiaoximen announced that starting today, to treat audiences in southern Shanghai, the theater is specially screening the lifetime masterpieces of the great slapstick king Charlie Chaplin: "The Woman of Paris," "Sunnyside," and "A Day's Pleasure," totaling ten reels, plus a Black Cat cartoon. Ticket prices remain unchanged, it is said.

The Mingxing Film Company announced that its long-renowned and unprecedented martial arts epic "Burning of the Red Lotus Temple" has received enthusiastic welcome from audiences. Ten episodes have already been continuously produced. The excellent business performance can be called second to none among domestic films. This is also a great honor for the company. Although imitators have emerged like a swarm, they ultimately cannot hope to reach its heights. Currently, the eleventh episode is more than halfway through production. Director Zhang Shichuan is working day and night to speed up production. Because this episode has many special effects and photography, the company's entire photography and painting departments have been gathered to work hard to complete it as soon as possible. The release date of the film is not far away, it is said.

Obituary 156

Mrs. Yu, the virtuous wife of Mr. Tan Haiqiu, a former compradore at HSBC, was a devout Buddhist and philanthropist. Unfortunately, she suddenly passed away due to a stroke on the 23rd of last month. Friends and relatives were shocked and deeply saddened by the news. The funeral is scheduled for today (the 13th) at Shenshi. The route will start from the residence on Jessfield Road, proceed via Avenue Road, Gordon Road, Connaught Road, Sanbanchang New Bridge, Hengfeng Road, and Guangzhao Road, directly to Guangzhao Villa, it is said.

Publishing News 157

The Lüde Bookstore announced that the store is organized by Esperanto scholars in Shanghai and specializes in publishing books in Esperanto and Chinese for the convenience of Chinese scholars. The first book, "Tales of Little Brothers and Sisters" by Grimm, has been published and sells for one jiao. The second and third books will be published continuously soon. The Kaiming Bookstore on Fourth Avenue is the main distributor, it is said.

Medical News 158

The Tianji Medical Clinic on Shilu announced that the clinic's "Lung-Shaped Herb" specializes in treating tuberculosis. It has been sold for more than ten years, and various circles recognize it as a rising force in the field of lung treatment. All kinds of old and new, stubborn and difficult-to-treat lung diseases, when treated with this herb, show immediate results. Although there are imitations on the market recently, their treatment effectiveness cannot compete, and the famous name of "Lung-Shaped Herb" is increasingly prominent and more respected by patients. Therefore, the sales volume in other areas is very high, and there is often a shortage of raw materials. In addition, the clinic has hired a medical expert specializing in chemical testing of our country's miraculous herbal medicines and has discovered many kinds with definite therapeutic effects. New medicines will be announced soon, it is said.
